<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">единогла́сный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedinoglásnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

***единожды.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:единожды.html>еди́ножды</a> (23709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">еди́но-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedíno-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жды</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ždy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единожды.html>еди́ножды</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jedínoždy</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>once, on one occasion <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:единожды.html>еди́ножды</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jedínoždy</b> v žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">only/just <b>once</b> in smb's life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:единожды.html>еди́ножды</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>jedínoždy</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">more than <b>once</b>; on several occasions</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>1x, one time as much

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">едино-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedino-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лицо.html>лицо́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">licó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:единоличный.html>единоли́чное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:решение.html>реше́ние</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jedinolíčnoje</b> rešénije</i> ― <span class="e-translation">independent/single-handed decision; one-man decision</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:единорог.html>единоро́г</a> (30793)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">едино-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedino-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рог.html>рог</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rog</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единорог.html>единоро́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jedinoróg</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единорог.html>единоро́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единорог.html>единоро́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единорог.html>единоро́гов</a></b>)

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">zoology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sea unicorn, narwhal</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственный</a> (499)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единство.html>еди́нство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedínstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-енный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jedínstvennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sole, only, unique</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> unique, exceptional, unparalleled</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">grammar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> singular</li></ol>

***единый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:единый.html>еди́ный</a> (1429)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Derived from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ѥдинъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jedinŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">odín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единый.html>еди́ный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jedínyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>united, unified, common, indivisible</li>
<li>one, single, sole
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:единый.html>еди́ный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jedínyj</b> denʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a single day</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единица.html>едини́ца</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jediníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:единственный.html>еди́нственный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jedínstvennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:едкий.html>е́дкий</a> (8296)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:едкий.html>е́дкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jédkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)е́дче</b>)

***ежели.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ежели.html>е́жели</a> (3722)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small> pronominal neuter form <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ѥжє</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ježe</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">who, which</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ижє</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">iže</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ꙗжє</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jaže</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">ѥжє</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ježe</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">li</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">interrogative particle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ежели.html>е́жели</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jéželi</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> if, in case
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ежели.html>е́жели</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подумать.html>поду́мать</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассмотреть.html>рассмотре́ть</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глупость.html>глу́пости</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Jéželi</b> podúmatʹ, da rassmotrétʹ, to vsjó éto glúposti</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">if we think about it and examine it, it is all nonsense.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ёж</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jož</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́вый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-óvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ежовый.html>ежо́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ježóvyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hedgehog
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ежовый.html>ежо́вые</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рукавица.html>рукави́цы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ježóvyje</b> rukavícy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">iron hand; iron fist; iron rule</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>hedgehog</b> mittens</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***ездить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a> (1291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*ězditi</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jézditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поездить.html>пое́здить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to go (by horse or vehicle), to ride, to drive</li>
<li>to come, to visit</li>
<li>to travel
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́зжу</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> москву́.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja částo <b>jézžu</b> v Moskvú.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I frequently go (travel) to Moscow. (abstract verb)</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лошадь.html>ло́шади</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jézditʹ</b> na lóšadi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ride a horse (generally, abstract verb)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поезд.html>по́езде</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>jézditʹ</b> na pójezde</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to go by train (generally, abstract verb)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>The verbs <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поездить.html>пое́здить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pojézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> are abstract verbs. Their counterparts, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поехать.html>пое́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pojéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, are concrete verbs.</li></ul>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́зжу</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:машина.html>маши́не</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>jézžu</b> na mašíne.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm going by car.</span></div></dd>
<dd>The subject has no definite destination in mind, and perhaps travels in more than one direction. Here, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́зжу</a></b> is from the abstract verb <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></b>.</dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́ду</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> москву́.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja <b>jédu</b> v Moskvú.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">I'm going to Moscow.</span></div></dd>
<dd>The subject has a definite destination (i.e. Moscow) in mind and the intention of going in a single direction. Here, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́ду</a></b> is from the concrete verb <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></b>.</dd></dl></dd></dl>
<ul><li>Imperfective compounds of <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></b> are formed from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезжать.html>выезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyjezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:приезжать.html>приезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prijezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.).</li></ul>

***езжать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:езжать.html>езжа́ть</a> (11626)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:езжать.html>езжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">jezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to go by vehicle, to travel <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">repeatedly or frequently</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>; <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/iterative_aspect" class="extiw" title="w:iterative aspect">iterative</a> of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>This is an iterative verb, and in standard language is conjugated only in the infinitive and the past tense.</li></ul>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jézditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
